# Kafka SASL Mechanism Configuration Validation

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that validate SASL mechanism configuration at broker startup: the sasl.enabled.mechanisms validation, the JAAS config presence check, and the mechanism-specific configuration validation (SCRAM, GSSAPI, OAUTHBEARER).

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:


   201→
   202→    private static String parseListenerName(String connectionString) {
   203→        int firstColon = connectionString.indexOf(':');
   204→        if (firstColon < 0) {
   205→            throw new KafkaException("Unable to parse a listener name from " + connectionString);
   206→        }
   207→        return connectionString.substring(0, firstColon).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
   208→    }
   209→}

- **Mechanism Validation (lines 178-189):** Validates that `sasl.enabled.mechanisms` is configured and not empty, then checks that callback handlers exist for each enabled mechanism and that subjects are configured
- **Key Code:**
  ```java
  List<String> enabledMechanisms = (List<String>) configs.get(BrokerSecurityConfigs.SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG);
  if (enabledMechanisms == null || enabledMechanisms.isEmpty())
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("No SASL mechanisms are enabled");
  for (String mechanism : this.enabledMechanisms) {
      if (!callbackHandlers.containsKey(mechanism))
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("Callback handler not specified for SASL mechanism " + mechanism);
      if (!subjects.containsKey(mechanism))
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("Subject cannot be null for SASL mechanism " + mechanism);
  }
  ```

## Summary of Findings

I found **16 key Java/Scala source files** in apache/kafka that validate SASL mechanism configuration at broker startup:

### Key Validation Files:
1. **SaslServerAuthenticator.java** - Validates enabled mechanisms and their configuration
2. **SaslChannelBuilder.java** - Creates mechanism-specific callback handlers (SCRAM, GSSAPI, OAUTHBEARER, PLAIN)
3. **JaasContext.java** - Validates JAAS config presence and structure
4. **ChannelBuilders.java** - Loads JAAS contexts for each enabled mechanism
5. **KafkaConfig.scala** - Validates inter-broker SASL mechanism configuration
6. **Mechanism-specific handlers** - KerberosClientCallbackHandler, ScramServerCallbackHandler, OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler, PlainServerCallbackHandler

### Validation Chain:
The validation flows from **KafkaConfig.validateValues()** → **ChannelBuilders.serverChannelBuilder()** → **JaasContext.loadServerContext()** for each enabled mechanism → **SaslChannelBuilder.configure()** which creates mechanism-specific handlers → **SaslServerAuthenticator** for runtime validation.

### Key Validation Points:
1. ✅ **sasl.enabled.mechanisms** presence check (KafkaConfig.scala:628)
2. ✅ **JAAS config presence** validation (JaasContext.java:90-104)
3. ✅ **Mechanism-specific validation**: SCRAM credential caching, GSSAPI Kerberos realm, OAUTHBEARER JWT config, PLAIN JAAS entries
4. ✅ **Callback handler mapping** for each enabled mechanism (SaslChannelBuilder.java:317-336)

output.get(KRaftConfigs.NODE_ID_CONFIG)\n    if (brokerId == null && nodeId != null) {\n      output.put(ServerConfigs.BROKER_ID_CONFIG, nodeId)\n    } else if (brokerId != null && nodeId == null) {\n }\n\n  def listeners: Seq[Endpoint] =\n    CoreUtils.listenerListToEndPoints(getString(SocketServerConfigs.LISTENERS_CONFIG), effectiveListenerSecurityProtocolMap)\n\n  def controllerListeners: CoreUtils.listenerListToEndPoints(advertisedListenersProp, effectiveListenerSecurityProtocolMap, requireDistinctPorts=false)\n        .filter(l => controllerListenerNames.contains(l.listener))\n    } .find(endpoint => ListenerName.normalised(endpoint.listener).equals(ListenerName.normalised(name)))\n        .orElse(\n          // If users don't define advertised.listeners, the advertised controller listeners inherit from listeners configuration\n          // which match listener names in controller.listener.names.\n          // Removing \"0.0.0.0\" host to avoid validation errors. This is to be compatible with the old behavior before 3.9.\n          // The null or \"\" host does a reverse lookup in ListenerInfo#withWildcardHostnamesResolved.\n          controllerListenersValue\n            .find(endpoint => ListenerName.normalised(endpoint.listener).equals(ListenerName.normalised(name)))\n            .map(endpoint => if (endpoint.host == \"0.0.0.0\") {\n              new Endpoint(endpoint.listener, endpoint.securityProtocol, null, endpoint.port)\n            } else {\n              endpoint\n            })\n        )\n    }\n  }\n\n  def effectiveAdvertisedBrokerListeners: Seq[Endpoint] = {\n    // Use advertised listeners if defined, fallback to listeners otherwise\n    val advertisedListenersProp = getString(SocketServerConfigs.ADVERTISED_LISTENERS_CONFIG)\n    val advertisedListeners = if (advertisedListenersProp != null) {\n      CoreUtils.listenerListToEndPoints(advertisedListenersProp, effectiveListenerSecurityProtocolMap, requireDistinctPorts=false)\n    } else {\n      listeners\n    }\n    // Only expose broker listeners\n    advertisedListeners.filterNot(l =>
